[USER] <teammate-message teammate_id="petit-chat" color="green" summary="Broadcasting Rule 305 proposal">
Here's my proposal for Rule 305:

**Rule 305:** When a proposal is adopted, each non-proposing player who cast a valid "for" vote earns 2 bonus points.

Right now, only the proposer benefits when a rule passes (+5 from Rule 216, +2 from Rule 301 if unanimous). Voters who help make it happen get nothing. This rule changes that — if you vote for a proposal and it passes, you earn 2 points.

[USER] <teammate-message teammate_id="petit-chat" color="green" summary="Broadcasting Rule 308 proposal">
Here's my proposal for Rule 308:

**Rule 308:** When a proposal is defeated, each player who cast a valid "against" vote earns 1 bonus point.

This is the natural counterpart to Rule 305, which gives +2 for voting "for" on adopted proposals. Rule 308 gives +1 for voting "against" on defeated proposals.
